SELECT TOP 1000 T.[OBJID]
            ,CASE T.[ERR_CODE] WHEN 0 THEN '正常' ELSE '异常' END ERR_CODE
            ,T.[ERR_DESC]
            ,CASE T.[PROC_STATUS] WHEN 0 THEN '等待' WHEN 1 THEN '执行' WHEN 2 THEN '完成' END PROC_STATUS
            ,T.[PROC_CREATE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_EXCUTE_TIME]
            ,T.[PROC_FINISH_TIME]
            ,T.[ORDER_TYPE_NO]
            ,T1.LOC_NO SLOC_NO
            ,T2.LOC_NO ELOC_NO
            ,T.[SOURCE_TYPE]
            ,T.[PALLET_NO]
            ,T.[SLOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[SLOC_AREA]
            ,T.[ELOC_TYPE]
            ,CASE T.[PALLET_TYPE] WHEN '1000 'THEN '载货' WHEN '2000' THEN '空载' ELSE '异常' END PALLET_TYPE
            ,T.[ORDER_TYPE_MODULE]
            ,T.[ROUTE_NOS]
            ,T.[PACKAGE_GUID]
            ,T.[TASK_GUID]
            ,T.[TASK_NO]
            ,T.[ELOC_AREA]
        FROM [dbo].[TPROC_0100_TASK_REQUEST] T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T1 ON T1.LOC_NO = T.SLOC_NO
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T2 ON T2.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO
       
      ORDER BY T.OBJID DESC

            ,T.[SLOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[ELOC_TYPE]
            ,T.[TRANSFER_TYPE]

            ,T.[ALL_ROUTE_NOS]
            ,T.[UNEXE_ROUTE_NOS]
            ,T.[CURR_ROUTE_NO]
            ,T.[PACKAGE_GUID]
            ,T.[CMD_REQUEST_ID]
        FROM [dbo].[TPROC_0300_CMD_FINISH] T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T1 ON T1.LOC_NO = T.CURR_LOC_NO
        LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T2 ON T2.LOC_NO = T.ELOC_NO

2018-09-27 16:43:15,701 [12] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetBillDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT CASE t1.ELOC_NO
           WHEN '00000000' THEN
            '立库'
           ELSE
            t3.loc_name
         END AS ELOC_NAME,
         T1.MATERIAL_NO,t1.product_grade,
          T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE1,
         CASE T4.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE
           WHEN 'I' THEN
            '入库'
           WHEN 'O' THEN
            '出库'
           WHEN 'M' THEN
            '移库'
           WHEN 'T' THEN
            '移载'
         END AS ORDER_TYPE_MODULE,
         T1.ORDER_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_BIN_NO,
         T1.ELOC_NO,
         T1.LIMIT_PALLET_ID,
         T1.LIMIT_PRODUCT_GUID,
         T1.CREATION_DATE,
         T1.DELETE_FLAG,
         T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
         T1.LINE_ID,
         T1.SORT_ID,
         T1.REQUIRE_QTY,
         T1.ACT_QTY,
         T1.SHIP_QTY,
         T1.BIN_ERR_DESC,
         CASE T1.LOCK_END_LOC
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '未锁定'
           ELSE
            '锁定'
         END AS LOCK_END_LOC,
         T1.Line_Status as LINE_NO,
         CASE T1.LINE_STATUS
           WHEN 0 THEN
            '等待'
           WHEN 1 THEN
            '下达'
           WHEN 2 THEN
            '执行'
           WHEN 3 THEN
            '完成'
           ELSE
            '取消'
         END AS LINE_STATUS,
         T1.LINE_STATUS STATUS
          FROM WBS_ORDER_LINE T1
          LEFT JOIN Psb_Material T2
            ON T1.MATERIAL_NO = T2.MATER_NO
          LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC T3
            ON T1.ELOC_NO = T3.LOC_NO
          LEFT JOIN WBS_ORDER T4
            ON T4.ORDER_NO = T1.ORDER_NO WHERE T1.DELETE_FLAG='N') TA
       WHERE    TA.STATUS >= 0    
        ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2018-09-27 16:43:16,215 [9] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetTaskDataTable
select TA.*
        from (SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                CASE WHEN T.TASK_STEP = '0000' THEN '等待' ELSE '执行' END TASK_STEP, 
                T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,T1.MATER_NO,1 USE_QTY
          FROM WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        UNION ALL
        SELECT T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.EMERGENCY,T.SLOC_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
                CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库' 
                ELSE '移库' END IO_TYPE,
                T.ELOC_NO,T.PALLET_NO,T.PACKAGE_GUID,T.ORDER_LINE_GUID,
                T.SORT_ID,T.CREATION_DATE, T.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,
                '完成' TASK_STEP, T.ROUTE_NOS,T.UNEXE_ROUTE_NO,T.FINISH_DESC,
                ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATERIAL_NO,
                1 USE_QTY
          FROM Z50_WBS_TASK T
          LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1
            ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
          LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2
            ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID ) TA
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE
参数：
@param0=Can not Find

2018-09-27 16:43:16,783 [14] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BillTaskCmdService.GetCmdDataTable
select ta.* from 
          (SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库'
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_STEP = '00' THEN '等待' ELSE '下传' END CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
      UNION ALL
      SELECT T.OBJID,T.TASK_GUID,T.TASK_NO,T.SLOC_PLC_NO,T.ELOC_PLC_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
           WHEN T.CMD_TYPE = 'M' THEN '移库' 
           ELSE '移载' END CMD_TYPE,
           T.PALLET_NO,T.ROUTE_NO,T.TRANSFER_NO,
           CASE WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '10' THEN '堆垛机' WHEN T.TRANSFER_TYPE = '20' THEN '输送线' 
           WHEN T.TRANSFER_NO = '30' THEN 'AGV' END TRANSFER_TYPE,
           '完成' CMD_STEP,
           T.CREATION_DATE,T.EXCUTE_DATE,T.FINISH_DATE, T1.ORDER_LINE_GUID
      FROM Z50_WBS_TASK_CMD T
      LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T1 ON T1.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID) ta
       WHERE  TA.ORDER_LINE_GUID = @param0   
      ORDER BY TA.CREATION_DATE
参数：
@param0=Can not Find

2018-09-27 17:02:18,415 [49] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.TaskService.GetCrnForkErrorStatus
 
        SELECT FS.CRN_NO,
              FS.CRN_FORK_NO,
              FS.TASK_NO,
              CASE FS.TASK_TYPE WHEN 'I' THEN '入库' WHEN 'M' THEN '移库' ELSE '出库' END AS TASK_TYPE,
                CASE WHEN T2.ERR_NAME IS NULL THEN '正常' ELSE T2.ERR_NAME END AS FAULT_NAME,
              FS.FROM_BIN,FS.TO_BIN,FS.ACT_POS_X,FS.ACT_POS_Y,
              FS.FIP_FAULT_NO,
              FS.FIP_DATE,
              FS.FIP_HANDLE_RESULT,
              CASE FS.FIP_FLAG WHEN 0 THEN '正常' WHEN 1 THEN '待确认' WHEN 2 THEN '已确认' WHEN 3 THEN '已处理' END AS FIP_FLAG
        FROM PEM_CRN_FORK_STATUS FS 
        LEFT JOIN PSB_CRN_ERR T2 ON FS.FAULT_NO = T2.ERR_NO
       ORDER BY FS.CRN_NO,FS.CRN_FORK_NO

2018-09-27 17:03:58,318 [48] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@CrnErrLog
SELECT T.*, T1.ERR_NAME,
              ISNULL(WT.PALLET_NO,ZWT.PALLET_NO) AS PALLET_NO,
              ISNULL(WT.SLOC_NO,ZWT.SLOC_NO) AS SLOC_NO,
              ISNULL(WT.ELOC_NO,ZWT.ELOC_NO) AS ELOC_NO
        FROM Z40_CRN_FORK_ERR_LOG T
        LEFT JOIN PSB_CRN_ERR T1
          ON T.ERR_NO = T1.ERR_NO
        LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK WT
          ON WT.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK ZWT
          ON ZWT.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
       WHERE   T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME >= @param0    AND  T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME <=1+  @param1    
         ORDER BY T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME desc
参数：
@param0=2018/9/27 0:00:00
@param1=2018/9/27 0:00:00

2018-09-27 17:53:32,635 [47] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.PageActionService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.PageActionService.GetUserPageActionList
 
      SELECT t1.* FROM SSP_PAGE_ACTION  t1
      INNER JOIN V_SSP_USER_ALL_ACTION t2 ON t2.ACTION_ID = t1.OBJID

@param1=1

2018-09-27 17:53:32,693 [47] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：

2018-09-27 17:53:34,284 [32] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbRI.SspPageMenuService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbRI.SspPageMenuService.GetEntityList
SELECT * FROM SSP_PAGE_MENU  WHERE    PAGE_URL =  @param0
参数：
@param0=PLUGINS/JHWMS/BILLMANAGER/OUTPUT/SEARCHBILLOUTPUT.ASPX

      INNER JOIN V_SSP_USER_ALL_ACTION t2 ON t2.ACTION_ID = t1.OBJID

2018-09-27 17:53:34,400 [32] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.OutputService.GetBillOutputData
SELECT CASE TL.LINE_STATUS
            WHEN 0 THEN
             '未执行'
            WHEN 1 THEN
             '已下达'
            WHEN 2 THEN
             '执行中'
            WHEN 3 THEN
             '已完成'
            ELSE
             '已取消'
          END AS STATUS_NAME, T1.*, TL.*,
         CASE
           WHEN SL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.SLOC_NO
           ELSE
            SL.LOC_NAME
         END AS SLOC_NAME,
         CASE
           WHEN EL.LOC_NAME IS NULL THEN
            TL.ELOC_NO
           ELSE
            EL.LOC_NAME
         END AS ELOC_NAME
    FROM WBS_ORDER T1
   INNER JOIN WBS_ORDER_LINE TL
      ON T1.ORDER_NO = TL.ORDER_NO
     AND TL.DELETE_FLAG = 'N'
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC SL
      ON TL.SLOC_NO = SL.LOC_NO
    LEFT JOIN PSB_LOC EL
      ON TL.ELOC_NO = EL.LOC_NO
   WHERE TL.LINE_STATUS < 3
     AND TL.REQUIRE_QTY > TL.SHIP_QTY
     AND T1.ORDER_TYPE_MODULE = 'O'
         
      ORDER BY TL.CREATION_DATE DESC
参数：
